## צֵאָה (id: 006100000000000)

צֵאָה
=====

צֵאָה (H6627)

noun f · צֹאָה · צֹאִי

Body Products

excrement, dung \= excrement; ◄ produced by humans and animals; ► source of pollution and impurity; ≈ regarded as filthy

[DEU 23:14](https://ref.ly/Deut23:14) · [EZK 4:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:12)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 23:14; Ezekiel 4:12


## צֹאָה (id: 006101000000000)

צֹאָה
=====

צֹאָה (H6675)

noun f · צֵאָה · צֹאִי

Body Products

excrement \= excrement; ◄ produced by humans; ► source of pollution and impurity; ≈ regarded as filthy and therefore associated with sinfulness

[2KI 18:27](https://ref.ly/2Kgs18:27)1 · [ISA 36:12](https://ref.ly/Isa36:12)1

Unclean

filth literally: excrement; hence: \= filthy substance; ► which renders people dirty and unclean; ≈ associated with sinfulness

[PRO 30:12](https://ref.ly/Prov30:12) · [ISA 4:4](https://ref.ly/Isa4:4) · [ISA 28:8](https://ref.ly/Isa28:8)

1 2KI 18:27 · ISA 36:12 MT\-Q \| MT\-K חראים

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Kings 18:27; Isaiah 36:12; Proverbs 30:12; Isaiah 4:4; Isaiah 28:8


## צֹאִי (id: 006102000000000)

צֹאִי
=====

צֹאִי (H6674)

adj · צֵאָה · צֹאָה

Unclean

dirty, filthy \= pertaining to being dirty; ≈ associated with sinful behavior

[ZEC 3:3](https://ref.ly/Zech3:3) · [ZEC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Zech3:4)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Zechariah 3:3; Zechariah 3:4


## צֶאֱלִים (id: 006103000000000)

צֶאֱלִים
========

צֶאֱלִים (H6628)

noun m

Plants

lotus plants \= thorny plants of about 1\.5 meter high, bearing small, yellow fruit; ◄ \|iZyziphus lotus\|i\*, found in the northern part of the Jordan Valley and in Samaria

[JOB 40:21](https://ref.ly/Job40:21) · [JOB 40:22](https://ref.ly/Job40:22)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Job 40:21; Job 40:22


## צֹאן (id: 006104000000000)

צֹאן
====

צֹאן (H6629)

noun c · צֹנֶה

Domestic Animals

flock, small cattle, sheep and goats \= group of small domestic animals traveling and feeding together; ◄ consisting of sheep and goats; ► hair or wool shorn for weaving into cloth; female milked for food; may be killed and eaten for meat; used as sacrificial animal; ≈ associated with large quantities and also with God's people, who are often seen as a flock with God as their shepherd

noun c

Names of Constructions

**Collocation:** שַׁעַר צֹּאן

Sheep Gate \= one of the city gates of Jerusalem, ► through which small cattle could be taken

=======

name

Names of Locations

Zaanan \= town, also known as Zenan; ◄ territory of Judah

Graham S. Ogden

## צֶאֱצָא (id: 006106000000000)

צֶאֱצָא
=======

צֶאֱצָא (H6631) — צֶאֱצָאִים

noun m · יצא

Exist

what comes from ..., what ... brings forth \= object which derives from or comes from another object, used for plants and, by extension, for humans

[ISA 34:1](https://ref.ly/Isa34:1) · [ISA 42:5](https://ref.ly/Isa42:5) · [JOB 31:8](https://ref.ly/Job31:8)

Relatives

offspring, descendants \= one's children including their respective offspring ◄ literally referred to as those who come forth from someone

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 34:1; Isaiah 42:5; Job 31:8; Job 5:25; Job 21:8; Job 27:14; Isaiah 22:24; Isaiah 44:3; Isaiah 48:19; Isaiah 61:9; Isaiah 65:23


## צָב (id: 006107000000000)

צָב
===

צָב (H6632)

noun m

Vehicles

cart, wagon \= vehicle; ► used for transporting goods and people

[NUM 7:3](https://ref.ly/Num7:3) · [ISA 66:20](https://ref.ly/Isa66:20)

noun m

Small Animals

dab lizard, thorn\-tailed lizard \= relatively large type of lizard, with a length of about 65 cm, a fairly thick, squat appearance, and a thick, short tail covered with spikes; feeds on desert plants;◄ \|iuromastyx aegyptius\|i\* or \|iuromastyx ornatus\|i\*, found in desert areas; ► unclean animal

[LEV 11:29](https://ref.ly/Lev11:29)

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 7:3; Isaiah 66:20; Leviticus 11:29


## צבא (id: 006108000000000)

צבא
===

צבא (H6633 · A6634) — צֹבֶה

verb · צָבָא

Serve

to serve, to work \= action by which humans serve a community

[EXO 38:8](https://ref.ly/Exod38:8) · [EXO 38:8](https://ref.ly/Exod38:8) · [NUM 4:23](https://ref.ly/Num4:23) · [NUM 8:24](https://ref.ly/Num8:24) · [1SA 2:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam2:22)

Serve

to muster, to conscript, to call to arms \= causative action by which humans gather other humans together ► to serve a community

[2KI 25:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs25:19) · [JER 52:25](https://ref.ly/Jer52:25)

Conflict

to fight, to wage war denominative of צָבָא: \= action by which humans engage in warfare

[NUM 31:7](https://ref.ly/Num31:7) · [NUM 31:42](https://ref.ly/Num31:42) · [ISA 29:7](https://ref.ly/Isa29:7) · [ISA 29:7](https://ref.ly/Isa29:7) · [ISA 29:8](https://ref.ly/Isa29:8) · [ISA 31:4](https://ref.ly/Isa31:4) · [ZEC 14:12](https://ref.ly/Zech14:12)

Graham S. Ogden

Celestial Bodies

host of heaven, sun, moon, and stars \= collective of all celestial bodies that give light; ◄ created by God; ► often worshiped by people, contrary to God's law; ≈ in Daniel 8 possibly used as a metaphor for the people of God

Deities

of Hosts, Almighty One literally: "YHWH (or one of the other names of God or a combination thereof) of Hosts"; hence: \= epithet of God with focus on his being in charge of the host of heavenly beings surrounding his throne, praising him, and carrying out his will in earth; ≈ as an epithet it relates to God's power and control of the cosmos as the divine king and warrior

## צְבָאָה (id: 006110000000000)

צְבָאָה
=======

צְבָאָה (H6643c)

noun f · צְבִי · צְבִיָּה

Wild Animals

gazelle \= small to medium sized plain antelope, inhabiting savannah plains and semideserts, reddish brown in color with almost white underparts, and small horns (with exception of female impala); long\-legged, graceful, and an expert jumper; lives in small herds; the female is sexually active at one year; high rate of reproduction; ◄ \|iGazella dorcas\|i\* or \|iGazella arabica\|i\*; ► clean and can therefore be eaten; ≈ associated with speed, grace, beauty, female sexuality, male virility, and fertility

[SNG 2:7](https://ref.ly/Song2:7) · [SNG 3:5](https://ref.ly/Song3:5)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Song of Songs 2:7; Song of Songs 3:5

צְבֹאיִם (H6636) — צְבֹיִם, צְבֹיִים, צְבֹיִּים

name

Names of Locations

Zeboiim \= town; ◄ located near Dead Sea; ► destroyed with Sodom and Gomorrah

[GEN 10:19](https://ref.ly/Gen10:19) · [GEN 14:2](https://ref.ly/Gen14:2) · [GEN 14:8](https://ref.ly/Gen14:8) · [DEU 29:22](https://ref.ly/Deut29:22) · [HOS 11:8](https://ref.ly/Hos11:8)

1 GEN 14:2 MT\-K צביים \| MT\-Q צְבֹויִים 2 GEN 14:8 · DEU 29:22 MT\-K צביים \| MT\-Q צְבֹויִם

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 10:19; Genesis 14:2; Genesis 14:8; Deuteronomy 29:22; Hosea 11:8


## צבה (id: 006112000000000)

צבה
===

צבה (H6638)

verb · צָבֶה

Shape

to swell up \= process by which parts of the human body increase in size

[NUM 5:27](https://ref.ly/Num5:27)

Shape

to cause to swell up \= causative process by which water causes parts of the human body to increase in size

[NUM 5:22](https://ref.ly/Num5:22)

Wish

to desire, to wish \= state/process by which humans or deities experience a strong desire to perform an event

[DAN 4:14](https://ref.ly/Dan4:14) · [DAN 4:22](https://ref.ly/Dan4:22) · [DAN 4:29](https://ref.ly/Dan4:29) · [DAN 4:32](https://ref.ly/Dan4:32) · [DAN 5:19](https://ref.ly/Dan5:19) · [DAN 5:19](https://ref.ly/Dan5:19) · [DAN 5:19](https://ref.ly/Dan5:19) · [DAN 5:19](https://ref.ly/Dan5:19) · [DAN 5:21](https://ref.ly/Dan5:21) · [DAN 7:19](https://ref.ly/Dan7:19)

## צָבוּעַ (id: 006115000000000)

צָבוּעַ
=======

צָבוּעַ (H6641)

noun m · צֶבַע · צִבְעֹון

Color

speckled \= state in which the skin of animal has spots, stains, and other irregular markings of skin

[JER 12:9](https://ref.ly/Jer12:9)1

noun m · צְבֹעִים

Wild Animals

hyena \= mammal with a big head and of which the front feet are longer than the hind feet; it has a brownish grey color with dark indistinct stripes that become spots and blotches on its neck; it has a stiff, upright mane that stretches from between its ears all the way down its back until the end of its tail; it feeds mainly on carrion and but occasionally goes hunting itself; lives in holes and hollows under logs but is also known to inhabit abandoned houses or tombs; produces wailing sounds; ◄ \|ihyaena hyaena\|i\*; ► probably unclean

[JER 12:9](https://ref.ly/Jer12:9)1

1 JER 12:9 RSV NIV NJB GNT CEV "speckled bird of prey" \= \[a] \| LXX NJPS NRSV REB "hyena" \= \[b] \| Hope (56ff,134\) prefers \[b], which is also supported by SIR.13:18 where the Hebrew version has צבוע and the Greek, ὑαίνης

Graham S. Ogden

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 12:9


## צבט (id: 006116000000000)

צבט
===

צבט (H6642)

verb

Non\-Possess

to pass, to hold out exact meaning unsure; probably: \= action by which humans stretch out their hand to other humans in order to give them something

1 PSA 112:4 The subject of this verse is ambiguous: RSV LXX "YHWH" \| NIV NJPS NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV "a person" \| the former interpretation is to be preferred as terms such as חַנּוּן and רַחוּם are attributes of God alone. 2 ISA 49:24 MT NJPS "victor" \| HOTTP\-C RSV NIV NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV עָרִיץ 3 ZEC 9:9 This passage is rendered differently in various translations. RSV, NRSV, NJPS suggest "triumphant," NJB has "vindicated," REB has "his cause won." These all relate to an aspect of meaning, "victorious." Other versions (KJV, NIV, NAB etc.) prefer the traditional "just."

## צדק (id: 006136000000000)

צדק
===

צדק (H6663)

verb · צַדִּיק · צֶדֶק · צְדָקָה · צָדֹוק · צִדְקִיָּה

Innocent

to be righteous, to prove to be righteous, to be just, to be in the right, to be innocent \= state or process by which humans and deities are found to conform to an accepted code of behavior

[GEN 38:26](https://ref.ly/Gen38:26) · [JOB 4:17](https://ref.ly/Job4:17) · [JOB 9:2](https://ref.ly/Job9:2) · [JOB 9:15](https://ref.ly/Job9:15) · [JOB 9:20](https://ref.ly/Job9:20) · [JOB 10:15](https://ref.ly/Job10:15) · [JOB 11:2](https://ref.ly/Job11:2) · [JOB 13:18](https://ref.ly/Job13:18) · [JOB 15:14](https://ref.ly/Job15:14) · [JOB 22:3](https://ref.ly/Job22:3) · [JOB 25:4](https://ref.ly/Job25:4) · [JOB 33:12](https://ref.ly/Job33:12) · [JOB 34:5](https://ref.ly/Job34:5) · [JOB 35:7](https://ref.ly/Job35:7) · [JOB 40:8](https://ref.ly/Job40:8) · [PSA 51:6](https://ref.ly/Ps51:6) · [PSA 143:2](https://ref.ly/Ps143:2) · [ISA 43:9](https://ref.ly/Isa43:9) · [ISA 43:26](https://ref.ly/Isa43:26) · [ISA 45:25](https://ref.ly/Isa45:25) · [EZK 16:52](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:52)

Innocent

to clear oneself, to justify oneself \= action by which humans make an effort to ensure that they are found to conform to an accepted code of behavior

[GEN 44:16](https://ref.ly/Gen44:16) · [JOB 32:2](https://ref.ly/Job32:2) · [JER 3:11](https://ref.ly/Jer3:11)

Innocent

to clear, to justify, to lead to righteousness \= causative action by which humans make efforts to ensure that other humans are found to conform to an accepted code of behavior, either in an absolute sense or relative to someone else

[JOB 33:32](https://ref.ly/Job33:32) · [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11) · [EZK 16:51](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:51) · [EZK 16:52](https://ref.ly/Ezek16:52) · [DAN 12:3](https://ref.ly/Dan12:3)

Innocent

to acquit, to declare innocent, to vindicate \= causative action by which humans or deities declare (other) humans to conform to an accepted code of behavior

[EXO 23:7](https://ref.ly/Exod23:7)1 · [EXO 23:7](https://ref.ly/Exod23:7)1 · [DEU 25:1](https://ref.ly/Deut25:1) · [2SA 15:4](https://ref.ly/2Sam15:4) · [1KI 8:32](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:32) · [2CH 6:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:23) · [JOB 27:5](https://ref.ly/Job27:5) · [PSA 82:3](https://ref.ly/Ps82:3) · [PRO 17:15](https://ref.ly/Prov17:15) · [ISA 5:23](https://ref.ly/Isa5:23) · [ISA 50:8](https://ref.ly/Isa50:8)

Good

to be restored \= causative action by which humans do what is needed to ensure that an object is be restored to an original and rightful state

[DAN 8:14](https://ref.ly/Dan8:14)

Right

to be right, to be just \= state in which an event is found to conform to an accepted standard

[PSA 19:10](https://ref.ly/Ps19:10)

צֶדֶק
=====

צֶדֶק (H6664)

noun m · צדק · אֲדֹנִי צֶדֶק

Good

just, accurate \= state in which a weight or measure is correct or accurate, in accordance with a standard

Right

righteousness, justice, deliverance, victory, vindication, prosperity \= pattern of behavior of humans or deities that is in accordance to the requirements of the divine law and generally aimed at establishing or restoring this pattern as a standard, which in certain cases requires a victory over evil and results in prosperity and happiness

## צְדָקָה (id: 006138000000000)

צְדָקָה
=======

צְדָקָה (H6666)

noun f · צדק

Right

righteousness, justice, deliverance, victory, vindication, prosperity \= pattern of behavior of humans or deities that is in accordance to the requirements of the divine law and generally aimed at establishing or restoring this pattern as a standard, which in certain cases requires a victory over evil and results in prosperity and happiness

## צִדְקִיָּה (id: 006140000000000)

צִדְקִיָּה
==========

צִדְקִיָּה (H6667) — צִדְקִיָּהוּ

name · צֶדֶק · יהוה

Names of People

Zedekiah \= man; ◄ son of Chenaanah; ► false prophet; time of king Ahab

[1KI 22:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:11) · [1KI 22:24](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:24) · [2CH 18:10](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:10) · [2CH 18:23](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:23)

Names of People

Zedekiah \= man; ◄ third son of Josiah; former name was Mattaniah; ► described as one "who did evil in the sight of the Lord"; uncle of King Jehoiachin; Nebuchadnezzar of Babylon appointed him king of Judah (597–587\) following Jehoiachin's rebellion; he too rebelled against Babylon and was eventually taken captive to Babylon, his sons were killed and his own eyes put out; contemporary of Jeremiah

Speak

to be commanded, ordered \= causative action with which a person is instructed how to behave or respond to a situation by a higher authority, either human or divine

[GEN 45:19](https://ref.ly/Gen45:19) · [EXO 34:34](https://ref.ly/Exod34:34) · [LEV 8:35](https://ref.ly/Lev8:35) · [LEV 10:13](https://ref.ly/Lev10:13) · [NUM 3:16](https://ref.ly/Num3:16) · [EZK 12:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:7) · [EZK 24:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:18) · [EZK 37:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek37:7)

Happen

to summon, to command \> to show (strength) \= causative action by which God or God's power is called up for rescue or refuge

[PSA 68:29](https://ref.ly/Ps68:29) · [PSA 71:3](https://ref.ly/Ps71:3)

Arrange

to set a house, affairs in order \> to prepare to die \= causative action with which a person puts one's house in order, that is, one's belongs and affairs, in anticipation of dying

[2SA 17:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:23) · [2KI 20:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:1) · [ISA 38:1](https://ref.ly/Isa38:1)

Leaders

commander \= someone who has been put into a position of authority, and is now able to prescribe the actions of others

[ISA 55:4](https://ref.ly/Isa55:4)

Mount Zaphon \= a mountain, identified with Jebel ʾel\-Aqraʿ ◄ in northern Syria, ► known by the Canaanites as the mountain of the gods

## צָפִיר (id: 006302000000000)

צָפִיר
======

צָפִיר (H6842)

## צרע (id: 006338000000000)

צרע
===

צרע (H6879)

verb

Impact

to suffer from a skin disease, to be affected by mildew \= state in which humans suffer from a condition that affects the skin, which probably covers diseases such as psoriasis, favus, leucoderma; ► a person who suffers from this disease is considered ritually unclean, and therefore unable to participate in worship; ≈ regarded as infectious, and seen as a curse and a punishment from God

Impact

## צרף (id: 006344000000000)

צרף
===

צרף (H6884)

verb · מַצְרֵף · צֹרְפִי

Test

to test \= action by which humans or deities examine the character of humans by having them engage in a certain activity, ◄ as a goldsmith tests the quality of a precious metal by smelting it in the fire

[JDG 7:4](https://ref.ly/Judg7:4) · [PSA 17:3](https://ref.ly/Ps17:3) · [PSA 26:2](https://ref.ly/Ps26:2)

Non\-Whole

to purge away \= causative action by which a goldsmith removes contaminants from a precious metal by smelting it in the fire; ≈ used as a metaphor for purging evil from the heart of humans

[ISA 1:25](https://ref.ly/Isa1:25)

Exist

to cast \= causative action by which a goldsmith creates an artifact from a precious metal by smelting it in the fire

[ISA 40:19](https://ref.ly/Isa40:19)

Test · Good

to refine \= causative action by which a goldsmith improves the quality of a precious metal by smelting it in the fire and so removing all contaminants; ≈ often used as a metaphor for purging evil from the hearts of humans

[PSA 12:7](https://ref.ly/Ps12:7) · [PSA 66:10](https://ref.ly/Ps66:10) · [JER 6:29](https://ref.ly/Jer6:29) · [JER 6:29](https://ref.ly/Jer6:29) · [ZEC 13:9](https://ref.ly/Zech13:9)

Test · Innocent

to refine \= causative action by which deities improve the character of humans by leading them through difficult circumstances, ◄ like a goldsmith improves the quality of a precious metal by smelting it in the fire and so removing all contaminants

[PSA 66:10](https://ref.ly/Ps66:10) · [PSA 105:19](https://ref.ly/Ps105:19) · [ISA 48:10](https://ref.ly/Isa48:10) · [JER 9:6](https://ref.ly/Jer9:6) · [DAN 11:35](https://ref.ly/Dan11:35) · [DAN 12:10](https://ref.ly/Dan12:10) · [ZEC 13:9](https://ref.ly/Zech13:9)

Test · True

true literally: tested; hence: \= state in which the words of deities have proven to be true and reliable, ◄ as a precious metal has been tested by a goldsmith and proven to be pure

[2SA 22:31](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:31) · [PSA 18:31](https://ref.ly/Ps18:31) · [PSA 119:140](https://ref.ly/Ps119:140) · [PRO 30:5](https://ref.ly/Prov30:5)

Professions

goldsmith, silversmith, refiner \= someone whose profession it is to work with precious metals, such as gold and silver

צרר
===

verb · מֵצַר · צַר · צָרָה · צְרֹור

Bind

bound up, wrapped up \= state in which objects are confined to one single place by a piece of cloth or something similar that is tightly wrapped around it, ► in order to keep them safely in place

Bind

to bind up, to wrap up \= causative action by which humans confine objects or masses to one single place by wrapping a piece of cloth or something similar tightly around it, ► in order to keep them safely in place
